I'm just going to go thru the Handbook and pull memeable concepts out

The Token Engineering Commons (TEC) decided to launch the Commons in 2 phases.

Voting in TEC Hatch DAO.

TEC Hatch DAO Mechanism

If the TEC Hatch DAO does not receive the Minimum Goal of *____* wxDAI after the Hatch period of *_* days, then the wxDAI will be returned to the address that sent it.

The Hatch Tribute

Advice Process

_26-Mar-21 04:19 PM_:

The Cultural Build

1. Clearly defined boundaries.

2. Congruence between appropriation and provision rules and local conditions.

3. Collective choice arrangements.

4. Monitoring.

5. Graduated sanctions

6. Conflict resolution mechanisms

7. Minimal recognition of rights to organize

8. Nested enterprises

Transparency Audits

I think rdfbbx mentioned that they would like to remake the whole Praise Bot with Java sometime ago.. I think the shift would make things neater. (A message from them a while ago in the PRAISEMERGENCY group suggested that there's a major boost up coming for the Praise Bot, with Dashboards, etc.) As for the bots I was working on, the call reminders won't break... But for the forms etc. we can do either of the following- - Switch to slash-command-bots (*this is a WIP by discord, and it might become really neat for forms, once they add ability of adding text) - Switch to JS. (Can certainly be an option, but involves re-writing a considerable amount of stuff) - I can make my own library based on discord.py (or wait for someone else to make one that's stable and maintained)

_10-Jan-22 06:50 AM_:

Hope it's no sacrilege to post this on the meme channel but since I don't do as well with memes as you talented folk, here's an update on the forum instead. Pipe in with thoughts or memes, as you see fit. [https://forum.tecommons.org/t/commons-upgrade-parameter-runoff-4-20-public-open-meets-ostrom-s-1m-hatch-fledge-fly/760/5](https://forum.tecommons.org/t/commons-upgrade-parameter-runoff-4-20-public-open-meets-ostrom-s-1m-hatch-fledge-fly/760/5)

Commons Upgrade Parameter Runoff - 4.20 Public Open Meets Ostrom‚Äôs ...

Same concern. The goal of launching with a higher market value of the TEC - given the intellectual capital, the know-how, our unique culture and community - has introduced this unintended consequence. (The original proposal before 420 had a market cap much more in line with the rest. This tweak was intended to see how much more value we can att...
